<h2>Wechat Post Format</h2>


<p>If you are going to produce a Wechat post, please follow the format below. If you are unable to provide a translation, please email us the original article and we will try our best to provide a translation. Due to the fact that the account is only allowed to broadcast one message per month, do note that not all articles will be broadcasted, however still published if it meets requirements.</p>


<pre><code>Featured Image

English Text

Blank line

Divider/Separating line

Blank line

Chinese text

QR Code to Wechat account

</code></pre>
